SELECT COUNT(*) FROM oseba acdt_o, upravna_enota acdt_ue WHERE (acdt_o.upravna_enota = acdt_ue.id_upravna_enota) AND (acdt_o.starost_d = 'C') AND (acdt_o.vozniski_staz_d = 'C') AND (acdt_o.strokovni_pregled_d = 'B');
